<html><head></head><body><div style="--fade-in-animation: fade-in-new-response 150ms cubic-bezier(0.3,0,0.8,0.15); animation: auto ease 0s 1 normal none running none; padding-top: 30px; position: relative; font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);"><div style="display: contents;">In JavaScript, the&nbsp;</div><span style="font-weight: 700;">decorator</span>&nbsp;syntax uses the&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">@</code>&nbsp;symbol followed by the name of a decorator function. This syntax is primarily used to modify or extend the behavior of&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">classes</span>&nbsp;and their members (methods, properties, and accessors).<span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 67.7188px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">GitHub</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+3</span></span></div></span></span></div><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">Basic Syntax<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">A decorator is placed directly above the target it is intended to modify:<span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 110.742px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">LogRocket Blog</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+3</span></span></div></span></span></div><div></div><div style="margin-block: 24px 32px; color: var(--jINu6c);"><div><div style="background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 16px 16px 4px 4px; overflow: auto hidden; padding: 12px 16px 0px;"><div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between;"><div style="font-family: var(--Eou8Yc); font-size: var(--GiToJf); line-height: var(--qWZYEc); letter-spacing: 0px;">javascript</div></div><div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; overflow-x: auto;"><pre><code><span>@decoratorName
</span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">class</span><span> MyClass {
  @decoratorName
  myMethod() {}

  @decoratorName
  myProperty = </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">'value'</span><span>;
}
</span></code></pre></div></div><div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px 4px 16px 16px; margin-top: 3px; overflow: hidden; padding: 0px 16px; height: 48px;"><div style="font-size: 12px;">Use code with caution.</div></div></div></div><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">Key Characteristics<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"></span></span></span></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Decorator Functions</span>: A decorator is essentially a higher-order function. When applied, it is called with specific arguments like the&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">value</code>&nbsp;being decorated and a&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">context</code>&nbsp;object containing metadata.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Decorator Factories</span>: If you need to pass arguments to your decorator, you use a factory—a function that returns the actual decorator function.</span><div style="margin-block: 24px 32px; color: var(--jINu6c);"><div style="background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 16px 16px 4px 4px; overflow: auto hidden; padding: 12px 16px 0px;"><div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between;"><div style="font-family: var(--Eou8Yc); font-size: var(--GiToJf); line-height: var(--qWZYEc); letter-spacing: 0px;">javascript</div></div><div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; overflow-x: auto;"><pre><code><span>@configurable(</span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">false</span><span>)
method() {}
</span></code></pre></div></div><div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px 4px 16px 16px; margin-top: 3px; overflow: hidden; padding: 0px 16px; height: 48px;"><div style="font-size: 12px;">Use code with caution.</div></div></div></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Current Status</span>: As of early 2026, decorators are in&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">Stage 3</span>&nbsp;of the&nbsp;<span><a rel="noopener" href="https://github.com/tc39/proposal-decorators" style="text-decoration-thickness: 1px; text-decoration-color: var(--JKqx2); -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1); text-underline-offset: 1px; outline: 0px;">TC39 proposal process</a></span>. They are not yet natively supported in all browsers and usually require a compiler like&nbsp;<span><a rel="noopener" href="https://babeljs.io/docs/babel-plugin-proposal-decorators" style="text-decoration-thickness: 1px; text-decoration-color: var(--JKqx2); -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1); text-underline-offset: 1px; outline: 0px;">Babel</a></span>&nbsp;or&nbsp;<span><a rel="noopener" href="https://www.typescriptlang.org/docs/handbook/decorators.html" style="text-decoration-thickness: 1px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Target Restrictions</span>: Standard JS decorators can only be used on classes and class members; they cannot be used on plain objects or standalone functions.</span><span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">2ality</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+9</span></span></div></span></span></li></ul><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; They are currently a&nbsp;</div><span style="font-weight: 700;">Stage 3 Proposal</span>&nbsp;in the&nbsp;<span><a rel="noopener" href="https://github.com/tc39/proposal-decorators" style="text-decoration-thickness: 1px; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"></span></span></span></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Standardization Status</span>: Stage 3 means the specification is complete and signed off, but it is waiting for "real-world" implementation feedback from browser engines before it can move to Stage 4 (Finished) and be officially included in a yearly ES release (like ES2026).</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; Modern libraries are now shifting toward the&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">Stage 3 ECMAScript Decorators</span>&nbsp;supported by tools like&nbsp;<span><a rel="noopener" href="https://medium.com/@mernstackdevbykevin/typescript-6-0-decorators-scalable-architecture-with-strong-typing-f5ce4a2e470b" style="text-decoration-thickness: 1px; position: relative; --m3c9: #e6e8f0; --m3c11: #e6e8f0; display: flex;"><div style="width: 652.438px;"><div><div style="display: contents;"></div></div><div dir="ltr" style="width: 652px; max-width: var(--CYi3c--fRcLaf,652px);"><div style="display: contents;"><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);"><div style="display: contents;">In Functional Programming (FP), the "decorator" concept is implemented through&nbsp;</div><span style="font-weight: 700;">Higher-Order Functions (HOFs)</span>&nbsp;rather than the&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">@</code>&nbsp;syntax used in classes. While the official ECMAScript proposal currently only supports the&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">@</code>&nbsp;syntax for classes and their members, the functional pattern of decorating functions is a core part of JS development.<span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 109.305px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">Stack Overflow</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+3</span></span></div></span></span></div><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">The Functional Decorator Pattern<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">In FP, a decorator is a function that takes another function as an argument and returns a new version of that function with enhanced behavior.<span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 70.8359px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">Medium</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+1</span></span></div></span></span></div><div></div><div style="margin-block: 24px 32px; color: var(--jINu6c);"><div><div style="background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 16px 16px 4px 4px; overflow: auto hidden; padding: 12px 16px 0px;"><div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between;"><div style="font-family: var(--Eou8Yc); font-size: var(--GiToJf); line-height: var(--qWZYEc); letter-spacing: 0px;">javascript</div></div><div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; overflow-x: auto;"><pre><code><span style="color: rgb(154, 160, 166); font-style: italic;">// A simple decorator (HOF)</span><span>
</span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">const</span><span> withLogging = (fn) =&gt; {
  </span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">return</span><span> (...args) =&gt; {
    console.log(</span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">`Calling ${</span><span>fn.name</span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">} with:`</span><span>, args);
    </span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">return</span><span> fn(...args);
  };
};

</span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">const</span><span> add = (a, b) =&gt; a + b;

</span><span style="color: rgb(154, 160, 166); font-style: italic;">// "Decorating" the function manually</span><span>
</span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">const</span><span> decoratedAdd = withLogging(add);

decoratedAdd(</span><span style="color: rgb(250, 144, 62);">2</span><span>, </span><span style="color: rgb(250, 144, 62);">3</span><span>); </span><span style="color: rgb(154, 160, 166); font-style: italic;">// Logs: "Calling add with: [2, 3]" -&gt; Returns 5</span><span>
</span></code></pre></div></div><div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px 4px 16px 16px; margin-top: 3px; overflow: hidden; padding: 0px 16px; height: 48px;"><div style="font-size: 12px;">Use code with caution.</div></div></div></div><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">Key Differences in FP vs. Class Syntax<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"></span></span></span></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Syntax</span>: FP uses standard function wrapping (e.g.,&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">const newFn = decorator(oldFn)</code>), whereas class-based decorators use the declarative&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">@decorator</code>&nbsp;syntax.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Current Specification</span>: There is a separate&nbsp;<span><a rel="noopener" href="https://github.com/tc39/proposal-function-and-object-literal-element-decorators" style="text-decoration-thickness: 1px; text-decoration-color: var(--JKqx2); -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1); text-underline-offset: 1px; outline: 0px;">proposal for function decorators</a></span>&nbsp;that would allow the&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">@</code>&nbsp;syntax on standalone functions, but it is currently at an earlier stage than class decorators.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Immutability</span>: FP decorators typically return a&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">new</span>&nbsp;function, leaving the original one untouched, which aligns with the principle of immutability.</span><span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 104.883px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">Atomic Object</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+3</span></span></div></span></span></li></ul><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">Common FP Decorators<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">Many popular utility libraries provide "decorators" that you likely already use:<span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 103.344px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">Atomic Object</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+1</span></span></div></span></span></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;"><code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">memoize</code></span>: Caches the results of a function based on its arguments.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;"><code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">debounce</code>&nbsp;/&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">throttle</code></span>: Controls how often a function can be executed (common in UI events).</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;"><code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">curry</code></span>: Transforms a function that takes multiple arguments into a series of functions.</span><span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 64.1562px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">Reddit</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+2</span></span></div></span></span></li></ul><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">Would you like a more complex example, such as a&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">composition</span>&nbsp;of multiple decorators applied to a single function?<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; padding: 4px 20px 16px;"><div role="button" tabindex="0" style="align-items: stretch; border-radius: 9999px; color: var(--jINu6c); cursor: pointer; display: flex; justify-content: center; overflow: hidden; position: relative; background-color: var(--aYn2S); outline: 0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px; line-height: 20px; margin: 8px 16px;">Show all</span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div></div><div></div></div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div></div></div></div><div style="--fade-in-animation: fade-in-new-response 150ms cubic-bezier(0.3,0,0.8,0.15); animation: var(--fade-in-animation); padding-top: 30px; position: relative; margin-top: 24px; color: rgb(230, 232, 240); font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; white-space-collapse: collapse; background-color: rgb(16, 18, 24);"><div style="position: relative; padding-bottom: 10px; max-width: 652px; z-index: 1; margin-top: 0px;"><div><div style="display: flex; gap: 4px; margin-left: auto; width: fit-content;"><div style="display: flex; position: relative; overflow: hidden; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 24px 4px 24px 24px; padding: 12px 16px; width: fit-content; flex-direction: column; max-inline-size: 472px; margin-left: auto;"><div style="display: flex; flex-direction: row;"><span role="heading" style="-webkit-box-orient: vertical; -webkit-line-clamp: 2; display: -webkit-box; overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; overflow-wrap: break-word; font-size: 16px; line-height: 24px; white-space-collapse: preserve;">the at decorator for functions in js, like python</span></div></div></div><div style="text-align: right; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 12px; line-height: 16px;"></div><div></div></div></div><div></div><div style="font-size: 16px; font-style: italic;">Something went wrong and the content wasn't generated.</div></div><div style="--fade-in-animation: fade-in-new-response 150ms cubic-bezier(0.3,0,0.8,0.15); animation: var(--fade-in-animation); padding-top: 30px; position: relative; margin-top: 24px; min-height: var(--aim-container-min-height); color: rgb(230, 232, 240); font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; white-space-collapse: collapse; background-color: rgb(16, 18, 24);"><div style="position: relative; padding-bottom: 10px; max-width: 652px; z-index: 1; margin-top: 0px;"><div><div style="display: flex; gap: 4px; margin-left: auto; width: fit-content;"><div style="display: flex; position: relative; overflow: hidden; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 24px 4px 24px 24px; padding: 12px 16px; width: fit-content; flex-direction: column; max-inline-size: 472px; margin-left: auto;"><div style="display: flex; flex-direction: row;"><span role="heading" style="-webkit-box-orient: vertical; -webkit-line-clamp: 2; display: -webkit-box; overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; overflow-wrap: break-word; font-size: 16px; line-height: 24px; white-space-collapse: preserve;">the at decorator for functions in js, like python</span></div></div></div><div style="text-align: right; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 12px; line-height: 16px;"></div><div></div></div></div><div></div><div><div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div></div><div></div><div><div><div style="color: var(--m3c11,#eef0ff); position: relative; --m3c9: #e6e8f0; --m3c11: #e6e8f0; display: flex;"><div style="width: 652.438px;"><div><div style="display: contents;"></div></div><div dir="ltr" style="width: 652px; max-width: var(--CYi3c--fRcLaf,652px);"><div style="display: contents;"><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);"><div style="display: contents;">In JavaScript, the&nbsp;</div><code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">@</code>&nbsp;decorator syntax&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">cannot</span>&nbsp;currently be used on standalone functions. Unlike Python, where&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">@</code>&nbsp;works on any function, the current JavaScript standard only supports this syntax for&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">classes</span>&nbsp;and their members (methods and properties).<span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 109.305px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">Stack Overflow</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+3</span></span></div></span></span></div><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">1. Current Status (ES2026)<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">While class decorators have reached Stage 3 and are officially part of the language path,&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">function decorators</span>&nbsp;are a separate, much earlier-stage proposal.<span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 67.7188px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">GitHub</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+3</span></span></div></span></span></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">JavaScript</span>: Only supports&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">@</code>&nbsp;on&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">class</code>,&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">method</code>,&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">accessor</code>, and&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">field</code>.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Python</span>: Supports&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">@</code>&nbsp;on any function definition.</span><span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 67.7188px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">GitHub</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+3</span></span></div></span></span></li></ul><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">2. How to achieve "Python-style" decorators in JS<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">To get the same behavior as Python's&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">@</code>&nbsp;syntax for a standard function, you must manually wrap the function. This is the&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">Higher-Order Function (HOF)</span>&nbsp;pattern.<span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 57.4531px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">Medium</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;"></span></span></div></span></span></div><div></div><div style="overflow-x: auto; width: 652px; margin-block: 16px 24px; box-sizing: border-box; scrollbar-width: none;"><table style="border: none; border-collapse: collapse; table-layout: auto; width: 652px;"><tbody><tr><th colspan="undefined" style="border-bottom: 1px solid var(--gS5jXb); min-width: 4em; vertical-align: top; font-family: var(--LI4Bo); font-size: var(--Mhs7de); line-height: var(--XWv1if); letter-spacing: 0px; padding: 8px 16px 8px 0px; text-align: left;">Python Syntax (Native)<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"></span></span></span></th><th colspan="undefined" style="border-bottom: 1px solid var(--gS5jXb); min-width: 4em; vertical-align: top; font-family: var(--LI4Bo); font-size: var(--Mhs7de); line-height: var(--XWv1if); letter-spacing: 0px; padding: 8px 0px; text-align: left;">JavaScript Equivalent (Manual)</th></tr><tr><td colspan="undefined" style="border-bottom: none; min-width: 4em; vertical-align: top; color: var(--bbQxAb); font-family: var(--LI4Bo); font-size: var(--Mhs7de); font-weight: var(--ofwUBc); line-height: var(--XWv1if); letter-spacing: 0px; padding: 12px 16px 12px 0px;"><code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">python @my_decorator def my_func(): pass</code></td><td colspan="undefined" style="border-bottom: none; min-width: 4em; vertical-align: top; color: var(--bbQxAb); font-family: var(--LI4Bo); font-size: var(--Mhs7de); font-weight: var(--ofwUBc); line-height: var(--XWv1if); letter-spacing: 0px; padding: 12px 0px;"><code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">javascript const myFunc = myDecorator(() =&gt; { // logic });</code></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">3. Comparison of Implementation<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">A typical decorator in both languages follows the "wrap and return" logic, but the application differs:<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Python Implementation</span><span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"></span></span></span></div><div></div><div style="margin-block: 24px 32px; color: var(--jINu6c);"><div><div style="background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 16px 16px 4px 4px; overflow: auto hidden; padding: 12px 16px 0px;"><div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between;"><div style="font-family: var(--Eou8Yc); font-size: var(--GiToJf); line-height: var(--qWZYEc); letter-spacing: 0px;">python</div></div><div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; overflow-x: auto;"><pre><code><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">def</span><span> </span><span style="color: rgb(250, 144, 62);">log_call</span><span>(</span><span style="color: rgb(250, 144, 62);">func</span><span>):
    </span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">def</span><span> </span><span style="color: rgb(250, 144, 62);">wrapper</span><span>(*</span><span style="color: rgb(250, 144, 62);">args</span><span>, **</span><span style="color: rgb(250, 144, 62);">kwargs</span><span>):
        print(</span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"</span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">Calling function</span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"</span><span>)
        </span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">return</span><span> func(*args, **kwargs)
    </span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">return</span><span> wrapper

@log_call
</span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">def</span><span> </span><span style="color: rgb(250, 144, 62);">greet</span><span>(</span><span style="color: rgb(250, 144, 62);">name</span><span>):
    </span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">return</span><span> </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">f</span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"</span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">Hello </span><span>{name}</span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"</span><span>
</span></code></pre></div></div><div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px 4px 16px 16px; margin-top: 3px; overflow: hidden; padding: 0px 16px; height: 48px;"><div style="font-size: 12px;">Use code with caution.</div></div></div></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);"><span style="font-weight: 700;">JavaScript Implementation</span><span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"></span></span></span></div><div></div><div style="margin-block: 24px 32px; color: var(--jINu6c);"><div><div style="background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 16px 16px 4px 4px; overflow: auto hidden; padding: 12px 16px 0px;"><div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between;"><div style="font-family: var(--Eou8Yc); font-size: var(--GiToJf); line-height: var(--qWZYEc); letter-spacing: 0px;">javascript</div></div><div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; overflow-x: auto;"><pre><code><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">function</span><span> logCall(fn) {
  </span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">return</span><span> </span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">function</span><span>(...args) {
    console.log(</span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"Calling function"</span><span>);
    </span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">return</span><span> fn.apply(</span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">this</span><span>, args);
  };
}

</span><span style="color: rgb(154, 160, 166); font-style: italic;">// Cannot use @logCall here yet</span><span>
</span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">const</span><span> greet = logCall(</span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">function</span><span>(name) {
  </span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">return</span><span> </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">`Hello ${</span><span>name</span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">}`</span><span>;
});
</span></code></pre></div></div><div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px 4px 16px 16px; margin-top: 3px; overflow: hidden; padding: 0px 16px; height: 48px;"><div style="font-size: 12px;">Use code with caution.</div></div></div></div><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">4. Why the difference?<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">The main technical hurdle for JS function decorators is&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">hoisting</span>. Standard function declarations in JS are hoisted to the top of their scope. Applying a decorator at the moment of declaration creates complex "chicken-and-egg" problems for the JS engine that Python (which does not hoist in the same way) does not face.<span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 66.1797px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">GitHub</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+1</span></span></div></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Summary</span>: If you want to use the&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">@</code>&nbsp;symbol today, you must wrap your function inside a&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">class method</span>. Otherwise, you must use standard function wrapping as a replacement for Python's "pie" syntax.<span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 54.0859px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">Axentix</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;"></span></span></div></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">Would you like to see how to configure&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">Babel</span>&nbsp;or&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">TypeScript</span>&nbsp;to enable the latest Stage 3 class decorators in your project?<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"></span></span></span></div><div></div><div><div style="clear: both; display: flex; flex-flow: wrap; row-gap: 16px; margin-block: 18px 0px; justify-content: space-between;"><div style="display: contents;"></div><div style="display: flex; gap: 4px; flex-shrink: 1; width: 652px; align-items: center;"><div style="display: flex; <html><head></head><body><div style="position: relative; padding-bottom: 10px; max-width: 652px; z-index: 1; margin-top: 0px; color: rgb(230, 232, 240); font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; flex-direction: row;"><span role="heading" style="-webkit-box-orient: vertical; -webkit-line-clamp: 2; display: -webkit-box; overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; overflow-wrap: break-word; font-size: 16px; line-height: 24px; white-space-collapse: preserve;">what are the most popular features after es6</span></div></div></div><div style="text-align: right; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 12px; line-height: 16px;"></div><div></div></div></div><div style="color: rgb(230, 232, 240); font-size: 14px; white-space-collapse: collapse; background-color: rgb(16, 18, 24);"><div><div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div></div><div></div><div><div><div style="color: var(--m3c11,#eef0ff); position: relative; --m3c9: #e6e8f0; --m3c11: #e6e8f0; display: flex;"><div style="width: 652.438px;"><div><div style="display: contents;"></div></div><div dir="ltr" style="width: 652px; max-width: var(--CYi3c--fRcLaf,652px);"><div style="display: contents;"><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);"><div style="display: contents;">Since the landmark release of ES6 in 2015, JavaScript has moved to an annual release cycle, introducing smaller but highly impactful features that simplify asynchronous code and data manipulation. The most popular additions since then include:</div><span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"></span></span></span></div><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">Essential Productivity Features<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"></span></span></span></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Async/Await (ES2017):</span>&nbsp;Perhaps the most significant post-ES6 feature, it allows you to write asynchronous code that looks and behaves like synchronous code, effectively replacing complex&nbsp;<span><a rel="noopener" href="https://academy.binary-studio.com/blog/the-long-path-of-java-script-from-es6-until-today/" style="text-decoration-thickness: 1px; text-decoration-color: var(--JKqx2); -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1); text-underline-offset: 1px; outline: 0px;">Promise chaining</a></span>.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Optional Chaining (<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">?.</code>) (ES2020):</span>&nbsp;Allows you to safely access deeply nested object properties without having to manually check if each level exists, preventing "cannot read property of undefined" errors.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Nullish Coalescing (<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">??</code>) (ES2020):</span>&nbsp;A logical operator that returns its right-hand side operand when its left-hand side is&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">null</code>&nbsp;or&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">undefined</code>, providing a safer alternative to&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">||</code>&nbsp;for setting&nbsp;<span><a rel="noopener" href="https://dev.to/carlillo/es2020-features-in-simple-examples-1513" style="text-decoration-thickness: 1px; text-decoration-color: var(--JKqx2); -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1); text-underline-offset: 1px; outline: 0px;">default values</a></span>.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Object.entries() and Object.values() (ES2017):</span>&nbsp;These methods make it much easier to iterate over objects by returning arrays of an&nbsp;<span><a rel="noopener" href="https://medium.com/@ratan.kumar67890/javascript-features-introduced-after-es6-2015-9e17fddbac0e" style="text-decoration-thickness: 1px; text-decoration-color: var(--JKqx2); -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1); text-underline-offset: 1px; outline: 0px;">object’s own enumerable properties</a></span>.</span><span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"></span></span></span></li></ul><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">Modern Data &amp; Logic Improvements<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"></span></span></span></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Object.groupBy() (ES2024):</span>&nbsp;A powerful new method that groups elements of an array into an object based on a&nbsp;<span><a rel="noopener" href="https://medium.com/@shoyshai/modern-javascript-es2024-features-every-developer-should-know-98956a7f4f05" style="text-decoration-thickness: 1px; text-decoration-color: var(--JKqx2); -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1); text-underline-offset: 1px; outline: 0px;">provided callback function</a></span>.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">New Set Methods (ES2025):</span>&nbsp;Standardized math-like operations for Sets, including&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">.intersection()</code>,&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">.union()</code>, and&nbsp;<span><a rel="noopener" href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=1-cjrEMj_us" style="text-decoration-thickness: 1px; text-decoration-color: var(--JKqx2); -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1); text-underline-offset: 1px; outline: 0px;"><code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">.difference()</code></a></span>.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Immutable Array Methods (ES2023):</span>&nbsp;Methods like&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">.toSorted()</code>,&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">.toReversed()</code>, and&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">.toSpliced()</code>&nbsp;allow you to manipulate arrays by returning a new copy instead of&nbsp;<span><a rel="noopener" href="https://codewithrajat.medium.com/javascript-es2024-a-deep-dive-into-the-latest-features-402a2e8c5eee" style="text-decoration-thickness: 1px; text-decoration-color: var(--JKqx2); -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1); text-underline-offset: 1px; outline: 0px;">mutating the original</a></span>.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Top-Level Await (ES2022):</span>&nbsp;Enables the use of the&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">await</code>&nbsp;keyword at the top level of a module, removing the need to wrap initialization code in an&nbsp;<span><a rel="noopener" href="https://medium.com/@fakecoder.in/javascript-es2024-new-features-and-how-to-use-them-738d271b1e61" style="text-decoration-thickness: 1px; text-decoration-color: var(--JKqx2); -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1); text-underline-offset: 1px; outline: 0px;">async function</a></span>.</span><span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"></span></span></span></li></ul><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">Advanced &amp; Niche Features<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"></span></span></span></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"></div><div style="position: relative; direction: ltr; display: inline-block;"></div></span></span></span>, the maximum limit for the standard&nbsp;<span><a rel="noopener" href="https://medium.com/@waleedarshadawan/top-10-new-javascript-features-in-es2020-that-every-developer-should-know-4e0643c88573" style="text-decoration-thickness: 1px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">&amp;&amp;=</code>,&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Nullish Coalescing (<code dir="ltr" style="font-size: 14px; line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">null</code>&nbsp;or&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="font-size: 14px; line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">undefined</code>, preventing issues where&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="font-size: 14px; line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">0</code>&nbsp;or&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="font-size: 14px; line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">""</code>&nbsp;were incorrectly treated as "missing" values.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">||=</code>,&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="font-size: 14px; line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">&amp;&amp;=</code>,&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="font-size: 14px; line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">??=</code>)</span>: Concise shorthand for assigning values only when certain conditions are met, such as setting default configurations.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Private Class Fields (<code dir="ltr" style="font-size: 14px; line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">#</code>)</span>: Enables true encapsulation by prefixing properties with&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="font-size: 14px; line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">#</code>, making them inaccessible from outside the class.</span><span><span style="white-space: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 166.922px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">JavaScript in Plain English</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+3</span></span></div></span></span></li></ul><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 57.4219px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">toReversed()</code>, and&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="font-size: 14px; line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">toSpliced()</code>&nbsp;return a copy of the array instead of mutating the original, which is a core tenet of modern functional programming.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Array Grouping (<code dir="ltr" style="font-size: 14px; line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">Object.groupBy</code>)</span>: A long-requested feature that natively groups items in an array based on a callback function.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">New Set Operations</span>: Built-in mathematical operations for Sets, including&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="font-size: 14px; line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">union()</code>,&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="font-size: 14px; line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">intersection()</code>, and&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="font-size: 14px; line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">difference()</code>.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;"><code dir="ltr" style="font-size: 14px; line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">Array.prototype.at()</code></span>: Simplifies accessing elements from the end of an array using negative indices (e.g.,&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="font-size: 14px; line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">arr.at(-1)</code>).</span><span><span style="white-space: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 115.164px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">DEV Community</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+6</span></span></div></span></span></li></ul><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">Promise.all()</code>, this waits for all promises to finish regardless of whether they succeeded or failed, making it ideal for bulk API calls.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px;
