overflow: hidden; position: relative; --thumbnail-width: 82px;"></div></div></div><div style="border-top: 1px solid var(--Lm570b); margin: 0px 16px;"></div></li><li style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;"><div style="padding: 12px 20px; position: relative; overflow: hidden;"><a rel="noopener" href="https://dev.to/hreuven/javascript-in-2025-your-roadmap-to-modern-features-31ff#:~:text=Temporal%20API:%20A%20complete%20overhaul,JSON%20and%20other%20file%20types" style="text-decoration-line: none; -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1); position: absolute; inset: 2px; z-index: 1; outline: 0px;"></a><div style="box-sizing: border-box; display: flex; justify-content: center; gap: 8px; height: 100.375px; overflow: hidden;"><div style="box-sizing: border-box; display: flex; flex-direction: column; flex: 1 1 0%; position: relative; min-height: 0px; overflow: hidden;"><div style="font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.4; margin: 0px 0px 4px; color: var(--jINu6c); display: -webkit-box; -webkit-box-orient: vertical; -webkit-line-clamp: 2; overflow: hidden; white-space-collapse: collapse;"><span>JavaScript in 2025: Your Roadmap to Modern Features</span></div><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); margin: 0px 0px 8px; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.3; display: -webkit-box; -webkit-box-orient: vertical; -webkit-line-clamp: 2; overflow: hidden; white-space-collapse: collapse;">Sep 1, 2025 —&nbsp;<span>Welcome to the first article in our comprehensive series exploring the latest JavaScript features that are reshaping how we write ...</span></span><div style="align-items: center; align-self: flex-end; display: flex; margin-right: auto; width: 242px; margin-top: auto;"><div style="display: flex; border-radius: 50%; align-items: center; justify-content: center; width: fit-content; vertical-align: middle;"><div style="width: 16px; height: 16px; line-height: 16px; display: flex; flex-shrink: 0; align-items: center; justify-content: center; overflow: hidden; background-color: var(--EoKObe); border-radius: 50%;"></div></div><div style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; white-space: nowrap; color: var(--IXoxUe); display: flex; flex-direction: column; margin-inline-start: 8px;"><span style="align-items: center; color: var(--bbQxAb); font-size: 12px; letter-spacing: 0.1px; line-height: 1.3; display: flex;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; flex-shrink: 1; max-inline-size: 200px;">DEV Community</span></span></div><div style="margin-inline-start: 8px;"><div tabindex="0" role="button" style="margin: var(--z9dUe--aOgmJd,0); position: relative; display: flex; justify-content: center; align-items: center; cursor: pointer; z-index: 1; outline: 0px;"></div></div></div></div><div style="border-radius: 8px; flex: 0 0 82px; width: var(--thumbnail-width); height: 82px; overflow: hidden; position: relative; --thumbnail-width: 82px;"></div></div></div></li></ul><div style="position: relative; padding: 4px 20px 16px;"><div role="button" tabindex="0" style="align-items: stretch; border-radius: 9999px; color: var(--jINu6c); cursor: pointer; display: flex; justify-content: center; overflow: hidden; position: relative; background-color: var(--aYn2S); outline: 0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px; line-height: 20px; margin: 8px 16px;">Show all</span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div></div><div></div></div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div style="--fade-in-animation: fade-in-new-response 150ms cubic-bezier(0.3,0,0.8,0.15); animation: var(--fade-in-animation); padding-top: 30px; position: relative; margin-top: 24px;"><div style="position: relative; padding-bottom: 10px; max-width: 652px; z-index: 1; margin-top: 0px;"><div><div style="display: flex; gap: 4px; margin-left: auto; width: fit-content;"><div style="display: flex; position: relative; overflow: hidden; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 24px 4px 24px 24px; padding: 12px 16px; width: fit-content; flex-direction: column; max-inline-size: 472px; margin-left: auto;"><div style="display: flex; flex-direction: row;"><span role="heading" style="-webkit-box-orient: vertical; -webkit-line-clamp: 2; display: -webkit-box; overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; overflow-wrap: break-word; font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 24px;">advanced data handling? should the browser grow infinitely just to bundle some libraries inside?</span></div></div></div><div style="text-align: right; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 12px; line-height: 16px;"></div><div></div></div></div><div><div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div></div><div></div><div><div><div style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--m3c11,#eef0ff); position: relative; --m3c9: #e6e8f0; --m3c11: #e6e8f0; display: flex;"><div style="width: 652.438px;"><div><div style="display: contents;"></div></div><div dir="ltr" style="width: 652px; max-width: var(--CYi3c--fRcLaf,652px);"><div style="display: contents;"><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);"><div style="display: contents;">The short answer is&nbsp;</div><span style="font-weight: 700;">no</span>, the browser isn't growing "infinitely" to copy libraries. It’s actually a strategic trade-off: moving popular library features into the native JavaScript engine often makes the web&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">smaller and faster</span>&nbsp;rather than more bloated.<span><span style="white-space: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">Here is why "Advanced Data Handling" belongs in the browser:<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="white-space: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"></span></span></span></div><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">1. The "Library Tax" vs. Native Performance<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="white-space: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">When you use a library like&nbsp;<span><a rel="noopener" href="https://lodash.com/" style="text-decoration-thickness: 1px; text-decoration-color: var(--JKqx2); -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1); text-underline-offset: 1px; outline: 0px;">Lodash</a></span>, every single user must download, parse, and execute that extra code before your app even starts.<span><span style="white-space: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 65.7188px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">GitHub</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+1</span></span></div></span></span></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Zero Download Cost</span>: Native features like&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="font-size: 14px; line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">Object.groupBy</code>&nbsp;or&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="font-size: 14px; line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">?.</code>&nbsp;are already compiled into the browser’s engine (e.g.,&nbsp;<span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;">Chrome's V8</span>). They cost the user&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">0 bytes</span>&nbsp;to download.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Optimized Execution</span>: Browser engines can optimize native functions at the machine-code level far more effectively than they can optimize third-party JavaScript code.</span><span><span style="white-space: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 65.7188px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">GitHub</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+1</span></span></div></span></span></li></ul><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">2. Solving "Code Duplication"<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="white-space: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">Without native features, every website on the internet bundles its own slightly different version of a "deep clone" or "group by" function.<span><span style="white-space: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 63.0703px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">Reddit</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+1</span></span></div></span></span></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Example</span>: If 1,000 sites all use&nbsp;<span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;">Lodash</span>, your browser has to download that logic 1,000 times.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">The Solution</span>: By moving these into the JS specification (TC39), the browser downloads the logic&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">once</span>&nbsp;during an update, and every website can then use it without sending extra code over the wire.</span><span><span style="white-space: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 65.7188px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">GitHub</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+1</span></span></div></span></span></li></ul><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">3. The "Stage" Filter (TC39)<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="white-space: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">The&nbsp;<span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;">TC39 committee</span>&nbsp;doesn't just add everything. Features must go through a rigorous&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">4-stage process</span>.<span><span style="white-space: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 92.5547px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">The New Stack</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;"></span></span></div></span></span></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;">They only "promote" features that have already been "battle-tested" in userland libraries for years.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;">If a feature is niche, it stays in a library. If 90% of developers are writing the same utility function manually, it becomes a candidate for the language.</span><span><span style="white-space: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 49.7656px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">Reddit</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;"></span></span></div></span></span></li></ul><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">4. New Architectures: "Built-in Modules"<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="white-space: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">There is an ongoing proposal for&nbsp;<span><a rel="noopener" href="https://github.com/tc39/proposal-built-in-modules" style="text-decoration-thickness: 1px; text-decoration-color: var(--JKqx2); -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1); text-underline-offset: 1px; outline: 0px;">JavaScript Built-in Modules</a></span>, which would allow the browser to have a massive "standard library" that is&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">lazy-loaded</span>. You would only "pay" the performance cost for the specific parts you import, and the code would be shared across all websites you visit.<span><span style="white-space: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 52.4141px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">GitHub</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;"></span></span></div></span></span></div><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">Summary of the Trade-off<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="white-space: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"></span></span></span></div><div></div><div style="overflow-x: auto; width: 652px; margin-block: 16px 24px; box-sizing: border-box; scrollbar-width: none;"><table style="border: none; border-collapse: collapse; table-layout: auto; width: 652px;"><tbody><tr><th colspan="undefined" style="border-bottom: 1px solid var(--gS5jXb); position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"></span></span></span></th><th colspan="undefined" style="border-bottom: 1px solid var(--gS5jXb); min-width: 4em; vertical-align: top; font-family: var(--LI4Bo); font-size: var(--Mhs7de); line-height: var(--XWv1if); letter-spacing: 0px; padding: 8px 16px 8px 0px; text-align: left;">Third-Party Library</th><th colspan="undefined" style="border-bottom: 1px solid var(--gS5jXb); min-width: 4em; vertical-align: top; font-family: var(--LI4Bo); font-size: var(--Mhs7de); line-height: var(--XWv1if); letter-spacing: 0px; padding: 8px 0px; text-align: left;">Native JS Feature</th></tr><tr><td colspan="undefined" style="border-bottom: 1px solid var(--gS5jXb); animation: var(--fade-in-animation); padding-top: 30px; position: relative; margin-top: 24px;"><div style="position: relative; padding-bottom: 10px; max-width: 652px; z-index: 1; margin-top: 0px;"><div><div style="display: flex; gap: 4px; margin-left: auto; width: fit-content;"><div style="display: flex; position: relative; overflow: hidden; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 24px 4px 24px 24px; padding: 12px 16px; width: fit-content; flex-direction: column; max-inline-size: 472px; margin-left: auto;"><div style="display: flex; flex-direction: row;"><span role="heading" style="-webkit-box-orient: vertical; -webkit-line-clamp: 2; display: -webkit-box; overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; overflow-wrap: break-word; font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 24px;">for these "advanced data handling" functions, how are they implemented</span></div></div></div><div style="text-align: right; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 12px; line-height: 16px;"></div><div></div></div></div><div><div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div></div><div></div><div><div><div style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--m3c11,#eef0ff); position: relative; --m3c9: #e6e8f0; --m3c11: #e6e8f0; display: flex;"><div style="width: 652.438px;"><div><div style="display: contents;"></div></div><div dir="ltr" style="width: 652px; max-width: var(--CYi3c--fRcLaf,652px);"><div style="display: contents;"><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);"><div style="display: contents;">The implementation of "advanced data handling" features in modern browsers is a deep-reaching process that moves from high-level JavaScript definitions down to highly optimized machine code.</div><span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="white-space: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"></span></span></span></div><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">1. Implementation Languages<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="white-space: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">Browser engines like&nbsp;<span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;">V8</span>&nbsp;(Chrome/Node.js) or&nbsp;<span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;">SpiderMonkey</span>&nbsp;(Firefox) don't just write these functions in standard JavaScript. They use a tiered approach:<span><span style="white-space: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"></span></span></span></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;"><span><a rel="noopener" href="https://v8.dev/docs/torque" style="text-decoration-thickness: 1px; text-decoration-color: var(--JKqx2); -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1); text-underline-offset: 1px; font-weight: 500; outline: 0px;">V8 Torque</a></span></span>: Many new features, like&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="font-size: 14px; line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">Object.groupBy</code>&nbsp;and&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="font-size: 14px; line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">Array.prototype.toSorted</code>, are written in&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">Torque</span>, a domain-specific language created by the V8 team. It looks like TypeScript but is designed to be translated into efficient assembly code.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">C++</span>: Core logic that requires direct memory management or complex data structures is often implemented in&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">C++</span>.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">CodeStubAssembler (CSA)</span>: For performance-critical "hot" paths, engineers write low-level code that is very close to assembly to ensure maximum execution speed.</span><span><span style="white-space: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 110.016px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">Stack Overflow</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+3</span></span></div></span></span></li></ul><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">2. Strategic "Pre-processing"<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="white-space: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">To make functions like&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="font-size: 14px; line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">.toSorted()</code>&nbsp;or&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="font-size: 14px; line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">.groupBy()</code>&nbsp;fast, browsers use internal tricks that a library cannot easily access:<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="white-space: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"></span></span></span></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Temporary Buffers</span>: For sorting or grouping, engines often extract values into a temporary, flat list in memory first. This allows them to ignore complex JavaScript "baggage" like prototype chains or getters/setters during the actual computation.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Memory Pre-allocation</span>: Unlike a polyfill that might grow an array one item at a time, the engine can often look at the input size and pre-allocate exactly the right amount of memory on the system heap.</span><span><span style="white-space: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 110.133px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">Stack Overflow</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+2</span></span></div></span></span></li></ul><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">3. Optimization via "Elements Kinds"<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="white-space: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">The browser tracks exactly what is inside your data structures to choose the fastest implementation:<span><span style="white-space: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 64.3203px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">V8.dev</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+1</span></span></div></span></span></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Smi (Small Integers)</span>: If you group an array of only integers, the engine uses a specialized "fast path" optimized for numbers.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Double/Object</span>: If you add a string or a decimal, the engine "transitions" the data structure to a more flexible—but slightly slower—format.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Hidden Classes</span>: The engine creates internal blueprints (shapes) for the objects returned by&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="font-size: 14px; line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">Object.groupBy</code>. This allows it to access properties later without doing a slow "hash table" lookup.</span><span><span style="white-space: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"></span></span></span></li></ul><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">4. The Path from Proposal to Browser<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="white-space: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">Before these features land in the engine, they follow a strict lifecycle managed by&nbsp;<span><a rel="noopener" href="https://tc39.es/" style="text-decoration-thickness: 1px; text-decoration-color: var(--JKqx2); -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1); text-underline-offset: 1px; outline: 0px;">TC39</a></span>:<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="white-space: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"></span></span></span></div><ol style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 20px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: decimal;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Stage 1-2</span>: Experimental. Developers use&nbsp;<span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;">Babel</span>&nbsp;to transform new syntax into old code.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: decimal;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Stage 3</span>: Feature complete. Browser vendors start writing the&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">native implementation</span>&nbsp;(C++/Torque) behind an experimental flag.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: decimal;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Stage 4</span>: Standardized. The feature is enabled by default for all users, and the polyfills in your codebase can be safely removed.</span><span><span style="white-space: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 137.68px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">V8 JavaScript engine</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+1</span></span></div></span></span></li></ol><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">Would you like to see a&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">performance comparison</span>&nbsp;between a native function like&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="font-size: 14px; line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">Object.groupBy</code>&nbsp;and a manual&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="font-size: 14px; line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">reduce</code>&nbsp;implementation?<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="white-space: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"></span></span></span></div><div></div><div><div style="clear: both; display: flex; flex-flow: wrap; row-gap: 16px; margin-block: 18px 0px; justify-content: space-between;"><div style="display: contents;"></div><div style="display: flex; gap: 4px; flex-shrink: 1; width: 652px; align-items: center;"><div style="display: flex; align-items: center; justify-content: center; gap: 4px;"><div style="display: flex; inline-size: 44px;"><div style="position: relative; display: inline-flex;"><span style="inline-size: 20px; block-size: 20px;"><div></div></span></div></div></div><div><div><div style="display: flex; inline-size: 44px;"><div style="inline-size: 20px; block-size: 20px;"></div><div></div><div></div></div></div></div><div style="display: inline-flex; gap: 4px;"><div style="position: relative; display: inline-flex;"><span style="width: 20px; position: relative; display: flex; justify-content: center; align-items: center; cursor: pointer; z-index: 1; outline: 0px;"></div></div></div></div></div></div></li></ul><div style="position: relative; padding: 4px 20px 16px;"><div role="button" tabindex="0" style="align-items: stretch; border-radius: 9999px; color: var(--jINu6c); cursor: pointer; display: flex; justify-content: center; overflow: hidden; position: relative; background-color: var(--aYn2S); outline: 0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px; line-height: 20px; margin: 8px 16px;">Show all</span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div></div><div></div></div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div></div></div></div><div style="--fade-in-animation: fade-in-new-response 150ms cubic-bezier(0.3,0,0.8,0.15); animation: var(--fade-in-animation); padding-top: 30px; position: relative; margin-top: 24px;"><div style="position: relative; padding-bottom: 10px; max-width: 652px; z-index: 1; margin-top: 0px;"><div><div style="display: flex; gap: 4px; margin-left: auto; width: fit-content;"><div style="display: flex; position: relative; overflow: hidden; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 24px 4px 24px 24px; padding: 12px 16px; width: fit-content; flex-direction: column; max-inline-size: 472px; margin-left: auto;"><div style="display: flex; flex-direction: row;"><span role="heading" style="-webkit-box-orient: vertical; -webkit-line-clamp: 2; display: -webkit-box; overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; overflow-wrap: break-word; font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: 24px;">what about wasm, how much can wasm do compared with torque</span></div></div></div><div style="text-align: right; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 12px; line-height: 16px;"></div><div></div></div></div><div><div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div></div><div></div><div><div><div style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--m3c11,#eef0ff); position: relative; --m3c9: #e6e8f0; --m3c11: #e6e8f0; display: flex;"><div style="width: 652.438px;"><div><div style="display: contents;"></div></div><div dir="ltr" style="width: 652px; max-width: var(--CYi3c--fRcLaf,652px);"><div style="display: contents;"><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);"><div style="display: contents;">While&nbsp;</div><span style="font-weight: 700;">WebAssembly (WASM)</span>&nbsp;is excellent for heavy computational tasks, it cannot replace&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">Torque</span>&nbsp;for implementing core JavaScript features because it lacks the necessary "insider access" to the browser's memory and object structures.<span><span style="white-space: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"></span></span></span></div><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">The Key Difference: Insider vs. Guest<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="white-space: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">The fundamental distinction is that&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">Torque</span>&nbsp;is an "insider" language built specifically to write the engine's internal functions (built-ins), while&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">WASM</span>&nbsp;is a "guest" designed to run securely&nbsp;<em style="font-weight: inherit;">on top</em>&nbsp;of the engine.<span><span style="white-space: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 137.68px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">V8 JavaScript engine</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+1</span></span></div></span></span></div><div></div><div style="overflow-x: auto; width: 652px; margin-block: 16px 24px; box-sizing: border-box; scrollbar-width: none;"><table style="border: none; border-collapse: collapse; table-layout: auto; width: 652px;"><tbody><tr><th colspan="undefined" style="border-bottom: 1px solid var(--gS5jXb); min-width: 4em; vertical-align: top; font-family: var(--LI4Bo); font-size: var(--Mhs7de); line-height: var(--XWv1if); letter-spacing: 0px; padding: 8px 16px 8px 0px; text-align: left;">Capability<span><span style="white-space: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"></span></span></span></th><th colspan="undefined" style="border-bottom: 1px solid var(--gS5jXb); min-width: 4em; vertical-align: top; font-family: var(--LI4Bo); font-size: var(--Mhs7de); line-height: var(--XWv1if); letter-spacing: 0px; padding: 8px 16px 8px 0px; text-align: left;">V8 Torque (The "Insider")</th><th colspan="undefined" style="border-bottom: 1px solid var(--gS5jXb); min-width: 4em; vertical-align: top; font-family: var(--LI4Bo); font-size: var(--Mhs7de); line-height: var(--XWv1if); letter-spacing: 0px; padding: 8px 0px; text-align: left;">WebAssembly (The "Guest")</th></tr><tr><td colspan="undefined" style="border-bottom: 1px solid var(--gS5jXb); min-width: 4em; vertical-align: top; color: var(--bbQxAb); font-family: var(--LI4Bo); font-size: var(--Mhs7de); font-weight: var(--ofwUBc); line-height: var(--XWv1if); letter-spacing: 0px; padding: 12px 16px 12px 0px;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Object Access</span></td><td colspan="undefined" style="border-bottom: 1px solid var(--gS5jXb); min-width: 4em; vertical-align: top; color: var(--bbQxAb); font-family: var(--LI4Bo); font-size: var(--Mhs7de); font-weight: var(--ofwUBc); line-height: var(--XWv1if); letter-spacing: 0px; padding: 12px 16px 12px 0px;">Can directly manipulate JS objects, shapes, and prototypes.</td><td colspan="undefined" style="border-bottom: 1px solid var(--gS5jXb); min-width: 4em; vertical-align: top; color: var(--bbQxAb); font-family: var(--LI4Bo); font-size: var(--Mhs7de); font-weight: var(--ofwUBc); line-height: var(--XWv1if); letter-spacing: 0px; padding: 12px 0px;">Cannot directly access JS objects; must go through a slow "bridge".</td></tr><tr><td colspan="undefined" style="border-bottom: 1px solid var(--gS5jXb); min-width: 4em; vertical-align: top; color: var(--bbQxAb); font-family: var(--LI4Bo); font-size: var(--Mhs7de); font-weight: var(--ofwUBc); line-height: var(--XWv1if); letter-spacing: 0px; padding: 12px 16px 12px 0px;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Memory</span></td><td colspan="undefined" style="border-bottom: 1px solid var(--gS5jXb); min-width: 4em; vertical-align: top; color: var(--bbQxAb); font-family: var(--LI4Bo); font-size: var(--Mhs7de); font-weight: var(--ofwUBc); line-height: var(--XWv1if); letter-spacing: 0px; padding: 12px 16px 12px 0px;">Operates directly on the V8 heap where your variables live.</td><td colspan="undefined" style="border-bottom: 1px solid var(--gS5jXb); min-width: 4em; vertical-align: top; color: var(--bbQxAb); font-family: var(--LI4Bo); font-size: var(--Mhs7de); font-weight: var(--ofwUBc); line-height: var(--XWv1if); letter-spacing: 0px; padding: 12px 0px;">Lives in its own isolated sandbox with a private linear memory space.</td></tr><tr><td colspan="undefined" style="border-bottom: 1px solid var(--gS5jXb); min-width: 4em; vertical-align: top; color: var(--bbQxAb); font-family: var(--LI4Bo); font-size: var(--Mhs7de); font-weight: var(--ofwUBc); line-height: var(--XWv1if); letter-spacing: 0px; padding: 12px 16px 12px 0px;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Garbage Collection</span></td><td colspan="undefined" style="border-bottom: 1px solid var(--gS5jXb); min-width: 4em; vertical-align: top; color: var(--bbQxAb); font-family: var(--LI4Bo); font-size: var(--Mhs7de); font-weight: var(--ofwUBc); line-height: var(--XWv1if); letter-spacing: 0px; padding: 12px 16px 12px 0px;">Deeply integrated with the browser’s Garbage Collector (GC).</td><td colspan="undefined" style="border-bottom: 1px solid var(--gS5jXb); min-width: 4em; vertical-align: top; color: var(--bbQxAb); font-family: var(--LI4Bo); font-size: var(--Mhs7de); font-weight: var(--ofwUBc); line-height: var(--XWv1if); letter-spacing: 0px; padding: 12px 0px;">Traditionally manual memory management, though&nbsp;<span><a rel="noopener" href="https://v8.dev/blog/maglev" style="text-decoration-thickness: 1px; text-decoration-color: var(--JKqx2); -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1); text-underline-offset: 1px; outline: 0px;">WasmGC</a></span>&nbsp;is improving this.</td></tr><tr><td colspan="undefined" style="border-bottom: none; min-width: 4em; vertical-align: top; color: var(--bbQxAb); font-family: var(--LI4Bo); font-size: var(--Mhs7de); font-weight: var(--ofwUBc); line-height: var(--XWv1if); letter-spacing: 0px; padding: 12px 16px 12px 0px;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Performance</span></td><td colspan="undefined" style="border-bottom: none; min-width: 4em; vertical-align: top; color: var(--bbQxAb); font-family: var(--LI4Bo); font-size: var(--Mhs7de); font-weight: var(--ofwUBc); line-height: var(--XWv1if); letter-spacing: 0px; padding: 12px 16px 12px 0px;">Optimized for "micro-tasks" like getting a property or adding an array element.</td><td colspan="undefined" style="border-bottom: none; min-width: 4em; vertical-align: top; color: var(--bbQxAb); font-family: var(--LI4Bo); font-size: var(--Mhs7de); font-weight: var(--ofwUBc); line-height: var(--XWv1if); letter-spacing: 0px; padding: 12px 0px;">Optimized for "macro-tasks" like video encoding or physics engines.</td></tr></tbody></table></div><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">Why WASM can't do what Torque does<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="white-space: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"></span></span></span></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">The "Boundary" Problem</span>: Every time you call a WASM function from JavaScript, there is a performance "tax" for crossing the boundary. For a core feature like&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="font-size: 14px; line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">Array.at()</code>, which might only take a few nanoseconds, the cost of just&nbsp;<em style="font-weight: inherit;">starting</em>&nbsp;a WASM call would be higher than the function itself.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Object Property Access</span>: WASM does not "know" what a JavaScript object is. To read a property like&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="font-size: 14px; line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">user.name</code>, WASM would have to call back into JavaScript, which is extremely slow. Torque, however, is compiled specifically to navigate these objects at machine-code speeds.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Data Types</span>: WASM is strictly limited to simple numbers (integers and floats). It cannot natively understand complex JS types like&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="font-size: 14px; line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">BigInt</code>,&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="font-size: 14px; line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">Symbols</code>, or&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="font-size: 14px; line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">Maps</code>&nbsp;without significant overhead, whereas Torque was designed to handle the entire JS type system.</span><span><span style="white-space: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 65.6641px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">Reddit</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+4</span></span></div></span></span></li></ul><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">Where WASM Wins<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="white-space: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">WASM isn't "worse"—it’s just a different tool. It shines when you have a&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">contained, heavy algorithm</span>&nbsp;that doesn't need to talk to JavaScript constantly:<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="white-space: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"></span></span></span></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Image/Video Processing</span>: Heavy math on a large buffer of raw numbers.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Game Engines</span>: Porting massive C++ or Rust codebases (like&nbsp;<span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;">Unity</span>) to the web.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Calculations</span>: Complex scientific or financial simulations where the speed of math is more important than interacting with the DOM.</span><span><span style="white-space: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 75.4531px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">SitePoint</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+1</span></span></div></span></span></li></ul><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">In short,&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">Torque</span>&nbsp;is used to build the&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">engine itself</span>, while&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">WASM</span>&nbsp;is used to build&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">high-performance apps</span>&nbsp;that run inside that engine.<span><span style="white-space: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 137.68px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">V8 JavaScript engine</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+1</span></span></div></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">Are you considering&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">porting a specific library</span>&nbsp;to WASM, or are you just curious about how these&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">low-level systems</span>&nbsp;compare?<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="white-space: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"></span></span></span></div><div></div><div><div style="clear: both; display: flex; flex-flow: wrap; row-gap: 16px; margin-block: 18px 0px; justify-content: space-between;"><div style="display: contents;"></div><div style="display: flex; gap: 4px; flex-shrink: 1; width: 652px; align-items: center;"><div style="display: flex; align-items: center; justify-content: center; gap: 4px;"><div style="display: flex; inline-size: 44px;"><div style="position: relative; display: inline-flex;"><span style="inline-size: 20px; block-size: 20px;"><div></div></span></div></div></div><div><div><div style="display: flex; inline-size: 44px;"><div style="inline-size: 20px; block-size: 20px;"></div><div></div><div></div></div></div></div><div style="display: inline-flex; gap: 4px;"><div style="position: relative; display: inline-flex;"><span style="width: 20px; height: 20px;"></span></div><div style="position: relative; display: inline-flex;"><span style="width: 20px; height: 20px;"></span></div><div></div></div><div style="display: flex; gap: 16px; margin-inline-start: auto; align-items: center;"></div></div></div><div></div></div><div></div><div style="display: contents;"><div><div style="inline-size: 1px; block-size: 1px; opacity: 0; overflow: hidden;"></div></div></div></div></div><div style="display: flex; flex-direction: column; width: 652.438px;"><div style="display: contents;"></div></div><div style="display: flex; flex-direction: column; width: 652.438px;"><div style="display: contents;"></div></div><div style="display: flex; flex-direction: column; width: 652.438px;"><div style="display: contents;"></div></div><div style="display: flex; flex-direction: column; width: 652.438px;"><div style="display: contents;"></div></div><div style="display: flex; flex-direction: column; width: 652.438px;"><div style="display: contents;"></div></div><div style="display: flex; flex-direction: column; width: 652.438px;"><div style="display: contents;"></div></div><div style="display: flex; padding-inline-start: var(--rhYkpc--jCcM0d,76px);"><div style="display: contents;"><div dir="ltr" style="color: var(--jINu6c); font-size: 16px; position: sticky; top: 100px;"><div style="position: relative;"><div style="border-radius: 20px; height: 439.156px; position: absolute; width: 372px; top: 0px; left: 0px; background-color: rgb(23, 24, 31);"></div><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; flex-direction: row; justify-content: space-between; height: 20px; z-index: 1; margin-left: -6px;"><div style="display: contents;"></div></span></div><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); display: flex; align-items: center; justify-content: center; font-size: 14px; padding-top: 1px;"><span>13 sites</span></span><div><div><div tabindex="0" role="button" style="margin: var(--z9dUe--aOgmJd,0); position: relative; list-style: none; position: relative;"><li style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;"><div style="padding: 12px 20px; position: relative; overflow: hidden;"><a rel="noopener" href="https://v8.dev/docs/torque#:~:text=Torque's%20expressiveness%20is%20sufficient%20to,automatically%20by%20the%20Torque%20compiler." style="text-decoration-line: none; -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1); position: absolute; inset: 2px; z-index: 1; outline: 0px;"></a><div style="box-sizing: border-box; display: flex; justify-content: center; gap: 8px; height: 82px; overflow: hidden;"><div style="box-sizing: border-box; display: flex; flex-direction: column; flex: 1 1 0%; position: relative; min-height: 0px; overflow: hidden;"><div style="font-size: 14px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);"><div style="display: contents;">If we ignore the "permission stuff" (sandboxing and security), the comparison between&nbsp;</div><span style="font-weight: 700;">WebAssembly (Wasm)</span>&nbsp;and&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">Torque</span>&nbsp;becomes a battle of&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">specialization vs. generalization</span>.<span><span style="white-space: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">Torque is built specifically to "glue" the high-level JavaScript language to the browser's hardware-level engine, while Wasm is built to be a portable, independent high-performance execution target.<span><span style="white-space: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 137.68px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; min-width: 4em; vertical-align: top; color: var(--bbQxAb); font-family: var(--LI4Bo); font-size: var(--Mhs7de); font-weight: var(--ofwUBc); line-height: var(--XWv1if); letter-spacing: 0px; padding: 12px 16px 12px 0px;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Type System</span></td><td colspan="undefined" style="border-bottom: 1px solid var(--gS5jXb); min-width: 4em; vertical-align: top; color: var(--bbQxAb); font-family: var(--LI4Bo); font-size: var(--Mhs7de); font-weight: var(--ofwUBc); line-height: var(--XWv1if); letter-spacing: 0px; padding: 12px 16px 12px 0px;">Statically typed but designed to handle JS's dynamic types (Smi, HeapObject).</td><td colspan="undefined" style="border-bottom: 1px solid var(--gS5jXb); min-width: 4em; vertical-align: top; color: var(--bbQxAb); font-family: var(--LI4Bo); font-size: var(--Mhs7de); font-weight: var(--ofwUBc); line-height: var(--XWv1if); letter-spacing: 0px; padding: 12px 16px 12px 0px;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Garbage Collection</span></td><td colspan="undefined" style="border-bottom: 1px solid var(--gS5jXb); min-width: 4em; vertical-align: top; color: var(--bbQxAb); font-family: var(--LI4Bo); font-size: var(--Mhs7de); font-weight: var(--ofwUBc); line-height: var(--XWv1if); letter-spacing: 0px; padding: 12px 16px 12px 0px;">Has first-class, zero-overhead access to the browser's GC.</td><td colspan="undefined" style="border-bottom: 1px solid var(--gS5jXb); min-width: 4em; vertical-align: top; color: var(--bbQxAb); font-family: var(--LI4Bo); font-size: var(--Mhs7de); font-weight: var(--ofwUBc); line-height: var(--XWv1if); letter-spacing: 0px; padding: 12px 16px 12px 0px;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Optimization</span></td><td colspan="undefined" style="border-bottom: none; min-width: 4em; vertical-align: top; color: var(--bbQxAb); font-family: var(--LI4Bo); font-size: var(--Mhs7de); font-weight: var(--ofwUBc); line-height: var(--XWv1if); letter-spacing: 0px; padding: 12px 16px 12px 0px;">Compiles directly to&nbsp;<span><a rel="noopener" href="https://v8.dev/docs/torque-builtins" style="text-decoration-thickness: 1px; text-decoration-color: var(--JKqx2); -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1); text-underline-offset: 1px; outline: 0px;">CodeStubAssembler (CSA)</a></span>, which is nearly raw assembly.</td><td colspan="undefined" style="border-bottom: none; min-width: 4em; vertical-align: top; color: var(--bbQxAb); font-family: var(--LI4Bo); font-size: var(--Mhs7de); font-weight: var(--ofwUBc); line-height: var(--XWv1if); letter-spacing: 0px; padding: 12px 0px;">Compiles to a platform-neutral binary format that requires a JIT or AOT compiler to run.</td></tr></tbody></table></div><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">Performance Profile<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="white-space: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"></span></span></span></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Torque</span>&nbsp;is unbeatable for&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">micro-operations</span>. When you call&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="font-size: 14px; line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">array.push()</code>, Torque handles the logic in a few CPU cycles because it already "lives" inside the array's memory structure.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Wasm</span>&nbsp;is superior for&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">sustained computation</span>. Once you are inside a Wasm module—doing heavy math or image processing—it avoids the "deoptimization" risks of JavaScript engines. However, even without security checks, Wasm suffers from a "marshalling cost" when moving complex data back and forth to JavaScript.</span><span><span style="white-space: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 139.945px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">V8 JavaScript engine</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+5</span></span></div></span></span></li></ul><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">The "Standard Library" Problem<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="white-space: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">One of the biggest differences is that&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">Torque is used to build the language itself</span>, whereas&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">Wasm is used to bypass it</span>.<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="white-space: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"></span></span></span></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;">If you want to add a new method to&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="font-size: 14px; line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">Array.prototype</code>&nbsp;that is available to every website by default, you use&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">Torque</span>.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;">If you want to run a C++ physics engine in a specific web app, you use&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">Wasm</span>.</span><span><span style="white-space: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 139.734px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">V8 JavaScript engine</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+2</span></span></div></span></span></li></ul><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">In short: even if Wasm had full system permissions, it would still be slower than Torque for&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">manipulating JavaScript objects</span>&nbsp;because it wasn't designed to "speak" the language of the browser's internal memory heap.<span><span style="white-space: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 95.5312px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"></span></span></span></div><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; The "Stone" vs. The "Standard Library"<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="white-space: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">The core of your argument—that JavaScript should be the "stone" or a set of critical primitives—is a direct critique of the&nbsp;<span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;">TC39 committee’s</span>&nbsp;pivot toward a "batteries-included" approach.<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="white-space: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"></span></span></span></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">The Problem</span>: Historically, JS lacked a standard library, forcing every developer to bundle&nbsp;<span><a rel="noopener" href="https://lodash.com/" style="text-decoration-thickness: 1px; text-decoration-color: var(--JKqx2); -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1); text-underline-offset: 1px; outline: 0px;">Lodash</a></span>&nbsp;or&nbsp;<span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;">date-fns</span>. This led to the "library tax" (size and parse time).</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">The Tradeoff</span>: By folding these into the engine, we reduce download costs but permanently increase the&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">complexity of the browser engine</span>. As you noted, the barrier to entry is now so high that creating a new, competitive engine from scratch is nearly impossible.</span><span><span style="white-space: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 113.961px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">The Mozilla Blog</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+1</span></span></div></span></span></li></ul><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">2. Syntax Sugar vs. Runtime Reality<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="white-space: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">You pointed out that many features seem redundant when paired with modern tooling:<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="white-space: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"></span></span></span></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Optional Chaining (<code dir="ltr" style="font-size: 14px; line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">?.</code>) &amp; Nullish (<code dir="ltr" style="font-size: 14px; line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">??</code>)</span>: While these provide safety, critics argue they encourage "lazy" data modeling. Instead of using a library like&nbsp;<span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;">Zod</span>&nbsp;to validate data once at the boundary, developers often scatter&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="font-size: 14px; line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">?.</code>&nbsp;everywhere, which can mask bugs and increase logic complexity.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Generators &amp; Yield</span>: These remain some of the least-used features in the language (often under 20-30% usage in surveys). They were added to solve asynchronous flows, but&nbsp;<span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;">async/await</span>&nbsp;largely rendered them niche "magic" that most teams avoid.</span><span><span style="white-space: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 158.492px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">State of JavaScript 2024</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+3</span></span></div></span></span></li></ul><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">3. The "Opinionated" Nature of Built-ins<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="white-space: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">Adding data-handling functions like&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="font-size: 14px; line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">Object.groupBy</code>&nbsp;or&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="font-size: 14px; line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">toSorted()</code>&nbsp;makes an architectural choice for the developer.<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="white-space: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"></span></span></span></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Functional vs. Class-based</span>: You rightly noted that&nbsp;<span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;">private class fields (<code dir="ltr" style="font-size: 14px; line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding: 2px 4px;">#</code>)</span>&nbsp;lean heavily into OOP, which feels contradictory to the massive industry shift toward&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">Functional Programming (FP)</span>.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Userland vs. Core</span>: When a feature is in a library, you can swap it if you disagree with its implementation. When it’s in the browser, you are stuck with its complexity and potential performance quirks forever.</span><span><span style="white-space: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 52.4141px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">GitHub</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;"></span></span></div></span></span></li></ul><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">Summary of the "Complexity Debt"<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="white-space: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">The "wise" tradeoff for browser vendors is usually&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">global efficiency</span>&nbsp;(saving petabytes of data transfer across the entire internet) at the cost of&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">engine maintainability</span>. However, for a developer who values language purity, this feels like turning a lean scripting language into an overloaded "everything-framework."<span><span style="white-space: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">Do you feel this "bloat" is making the web&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">less stable</span>&nbsp;as a platform, or is it primarily a&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">developer experience</span>&nbsp;issue that makes the language harder to learn?<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="white-space: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"></span></span></span></div><div></div><div><div style="clear: both; display: flex;
